## Timeline

- 2025-07-02: Introduced in House
- 2025-07-02 - Calendars: Placed on the House Calendar, Calendar No. 35.

- 2025-07-02 09:00:02 - Floor: The resolution makes in order a motion that the House concur in the Senate amendment to H.R. 1 and provides for one hour of debate.
- 2025-07-02 09:04:12 - Floor: By direction of the Committee on Rules, Ms. Foxx called up H.Res. 566 and asked for its immediate consideration.
- 2025-07-02 09:04:17 - Floor: Considered as privileged matter. (consideration: CR H3039-3059; text: CR H3040)
- 2025-07-02 09:05:33 - Floor: POINT OF ORDER - Mr. McGovern raised a point of order against the provisions of H. Res. 566 on the grounds that the resolution violates section 426(a) of the Congressional Budget Act. The Chair announced that the disposition of the point of order would be resolved by the question of consideration of H. Res. 566. The House proceeded with 20 minutes of debate on the point of order at the end of which the Chair will put the question on consideration.
- 2025-07-02 09:18:30 - Floor: Mr. McGovern moved On consideration of the resolution.
- 2025-07-02 10:57:58 - Floor: On consideration of the resolution Agreed to by the Yeas and Nays: 212 - 211 (Roll no. 186).
  - Recorded vote: House session 1, roll 186 (2025-07-02T14:57:58Z)
- 2025-07-02 10:58:02 - Floor: DEBATE - The House proceeded with one hour of debate on H. Res. 566.
- 2025-07-03 03:23:49 - Floor: On agreeing to the resolution, as amended Agreed to by the Yeas and Nays: 219 - 213 (Roll no. 189).

Res. 14, with the Senate amendment thereto, and to consider in the House, without intervention of any point of order, a motion offered by the chair of the Committee on the Budget or his designee that the House concur in the Senate amendment.
